country_event = {
    id = 18490001
    title = "The Conquest of Odiene"
    desc = "ODIENEKABADUGU"
    picture = "kabadugu_map"

    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		tag = KNG
		owns = 3769
		1896 = { empty = yes }
		year = 1848
		month = 5
		DJK = { exists = no }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

    option = {
        name = "We should flee, and fast!"
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					1896 = { empty = yes }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				1896 = {
					secede_province = THIS
				}
			}
		}
		DJK = {
			all_core = { remove_core = DJK }
			primary_culture = dyula

			add_accepted_culture = western_nigritic
			remove_accepted_culture = kurdish
			government = absolute_monarchy
                    activate_technology = flintlock_rifles
                    set_country_flag = using_foreign_weapons
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					owns = 3769
				}
			}
			owner = {
				3769 = {
					secede_province = DJK
					add_core = DJK
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					owns = 3881
				}
			}
			owner = {
				3881 = {
					secede_province = DJK
					add_core = DJK
				}
			}
		}

country_event = {
    id = 18490002
    title = "The Kong-Gwiriko War of $YEAR$"
    desc = "GWIRIKOCHANGE"
    picture = "kong_map"

    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
		tag = GUK
		BDN = { exists = no }
		KNG = { is_vassal = no exists = yes }
		year = 1850
		month = 2
		NOT = { has_global_flag = sw_set }
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

    option = {
        name = "For Gwiriko!"
		BDN = {
			all_core = { remove_core = BDN }
			capital = 1082
			primary_culture = gur
			add_accepted_culture = bambara
			remove_accepted_culture = kurdish
			religion = fetishist
			set_country_flag = animist_country
                    activate_technology = flintlock_rifles
                    set_country_flag = using_foreign_weapons
		}
		change_tag = BDN
		government = absolute_monarchy
		GUK = { all_core = { remove_core = GUK } primary_culture = ukrainian add_accepted_culture = siberian remove_accepted_culture = gur remove_accepted_culture = bambara }
		war = {
			target = KNG
			attacker_goal = { casus_belli = humiliate_no_infamy }
			defender_goal = { casus_belli = humiliate_no_infamy }
			call_ally = no
		}
    }

}

		tag = SOK

			owns = 1949
		}

		KBO = {
			OR = {
				owns = 1949
				owns = 1951
			}
		}
		NOT = { year = 1844 }
	}

		any_owned = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					province_id = 1949
					province_id = 1951
				}
			}
			secede_province = KBO
			add_core = KBO
		}
	}

		name = "Go to war to reclaim it..."
		prestige = 5

			target = KBO
			attacker_goal = {
				casus_belli = acquire_any_state
				state_province_id = 1947
			}
			defender_goal = {
				casus_belli = acquire_any_state
				state_province_id = 3756
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
    option = {
		name = "Try to do this peacefully."
		KBO = { country_event = 184824442 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				war = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
